International Commercial Telegram July 25th Reuters Special Commercial Report 25

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price Today is one hundred and thirty-eight shillings ten and a half pence, up half a penny.

London Silver Bar Today is stable, the spot and futures prices are both nineteen pence six eight seven five, up 〇 six two five from yesterday, it is heard that India will purchase, while China will sell.

Mountrie Silver Bar Futures opened steady, the December price is four four · nine five — four five · three 〇, the same as yesterday's price.

Exchange Rates

British-American The London foreign exchange market was quiet and mixed this morning. The price of the pound sterling, converted to US dollars, is still stable. The British-American exchange rate opened at five dollars and one and eighty-one two five cents, down 〇 three one two five from yesterday's US-British closing price, later the price stabilized, and closed up one two five, at five dollars and two and ninety-three seven five cents.

Securities

New York The stock market opened quietly, and prices fell slightly due to profit-taking by bulls. Trading was sluggish in the first hour. Yesterday, Chrysler Motor Company claimed that it could earn four dollars per share in interest, so today auto stocks were strong, and the stock market sentiment was also stable as a result. General Motors stock also followed Chrysler and strengthened. The closing price was 71, a net increase of one pound and six two five. Railways were stable, and copper mines and public stocks were looser. The New York stock market prices are listed on the left.

Cotton and Wheat

Liverpool Wheat Today's futures price for October at 1:00 pm was six shillings and nine pence seven five, up seventy-five.

Liverpool Cotton Market Today's US cotton futures were firm, with the October futures up eight tones, at six · seven three.

New York Cotton Market Rose due to purchases by peers. There was slight profit-taking before 11:00, but the pressure was extremely weak. The October futures price at noon was one two · five four, a net increase of eighteen pounds and tones from yesterday.

Chicago Wheat Opened stable due to favorable weather news for the bulls, but later turned loose due to profit-taking by bulls. The September futures price at noon was one 〇 three · five 〇, the same as yesterday's closing price.

Chicago Grains Initially very loose, later rose due to purchases by speculators. The September futures price at noon was eighty-seven · eight seven five, up seventy-five from yesterday. The New York commodity market prices are listed on the left.

Rubber

New York Today's rubber market was closed.

Recent War in Spain Government Forces Have the Upper Hand Reinforcements Are Being Sent to the Front to Prepare for an Attack Rebels Announce the Establishment of a Provisional Government 26

Madrid The recent war in the vicinity is actually a war between labor and the army. Those loyal to the government have the upper hand today. Five thousand militiamen from the provinces of Murcia and Valencia arrived in the capital in time to replenish the vacancies of those killed and wounded in the past few days, and morale was greatly boosted. After the rebel army approaching the capital was defeated, the troops, shock troops, garrison troops, and militiamen loyal to the government formed three columns, and then began to prepare to attack the rebel army in Zaragoza (Reuters dispatch on the 25th).

Guadalajara, Northern Spain Special dispatch from our agency, the reinforcements sent by the government have already arrived in this mountainous area, and many planes have also been concentrated and are waiting for orders. General Legmi, the commander of the front line, has set up his headquarters in the local post office, and personally went to the front line to inspect this morning, preparing to order an attack. Outposts have already made contact. It is generally believed that the decisive battle between the government forces and the rebel army is imminent. It is said that the government forces have gained the upper hand in the battles in the southern mountains after bombarding them with light artillery (Havas dispatch on the 25th).

Barcelona Four columns of government troops composed of garrison troops, shock troops, militiamen, and regular troops, as well as many armored vehicles and transport vehicles, left here for the Chai Valley today. People also automatically flocked to the temporary recruitment office to sign up for the army. The Catalan autonomous government today allocated a temporary military expenditure of three million pesetas to help with military expenses. The city is very quiet today, factories are unanimously closed, the power supply is cut off, and there are many electric poles lying down (National Telegraph on the 24th).

Madrid The Ministry of Interior announced today a military victory, saying that the rebel army could be conquered in a few hours, and that it has been confirmed that the rebel army's military expenses were provided by the Spanish millionaire Maki. The government forces are now firmly defending the mountain passes of Guadalajara, Chamucilla, and Navacerrada. The defense of the capital is very strong. After 3,000 government troops and 3,000 militiamen fought fiercely with the rebel army in the mountains north of the capital, they defeated the rebel army. The government forces have advanced 15 miles towards Segovia. The outcome of the battle will soon be known (National Telegraph on the 24th).

Rebel Headquarters on the North Road of Burgos The leader of the rebel army on the North Road, Mala, announced here today the establishment of a new Republican government of Spain, saying that the current government has collapsed, and more than eight-tenths of Spain's land has fallen into our hands. Free Spain should immediately restore its status as a civilized country, and nominated Gabaleras as the new president. Since hearing that the defense of the capital is strong, the rebel army has now postponed the attack (National Telegraph on the 24th).

Madrid Official sources recently stated that the government now controls 22 of the 50 provinces in Spain. The rebel army in the southeast is still stubbornly resisting in the Zhenchira area. The government forces have gone from the two cities of Cartagena and Aligande to suppress them. The radio station in Cadiz Port in the west is still in the hands of the rebel army. Many government-owned aircraft have recently flown to bomb it. The situation of the battle in the Guadalajara mountain area north of Madrid can be decided today. The government forces have been fighting there for four days and are exhausted. Today, fresh troops will be transferred to reinforce them, and the strength of the main army will also be strengthened. As for the positions occupied by the government forces, they have been stabilized since they captured the Lion Ridge yesterday. All the officers and soldiers on the front line are now allowed to use postcards and pencils to write letters home. This is the first time since the chaos occurred, which shows that the front line is not very tense. All the civil corps in the capital and the groups belonging to the People's Front have moved into various public agencies to work yesterday. Other major hotels, such as the Casino Hotel, the Royal Palace Hotel, and the Ritz Hotel, and magnificent private residences have been converted into the headquarters or hospitals of these groups. In addition, the problem of the people's food is still tight. The mayor of this capital recently stated that he has taken various measures and decided to distribute rations to the families of the civil corps who are serving on the front lines every day, the total amount of which is equal to the food needed by 20,000 people (Havas dispatch on the 24th).

(Paris) This question received a telegram from the US Embassy in Spain today stating that the government forces are fighting fiercely with the rebel army north of Madrid. The outcome is unknown. Foreign nationals in Madrid are gradually feeling uneasy (National Telegraph on the 24th).

Conflicting Military Reports Rebel Army on the North Road Repulsed While Peeking at the Capital Government Army Plane Shot Down on the South Road 27

Madrid Minister of the Interior Borges recently announced that the rebel army invading the Guadalajara Mountains (north of the capital) has been defeated by the government forces, and that the rebel army was also defeated near Guadalaville (Havas dispatch on the 24th).

Hendaye, France After several days of fighting, the city of San Sebastian in northern Spain has been recovered by the government army. It is learned that the number of deaths in this battle will be around 300 (Havas dispatch on the 25th).

Gibraltar The Spanish cruisers Quimera, Libertad, and Cervantes, and three submarines, recently sailed to a point several miles outside the port here, and immediately launched a surprise attack on the port of Ceuta in Spanish Morocco in North Africa. The port's batteries also opened fire in return. The Quimera was hit in the side and damaged. In addition, a government army plane was shot down and fell into the sea by the rebel army in the port of Algeciras in southern Spain (Havas dispatch from Agence France-Presse on the 25th).

(Paris) The Spanish Embassy in France recently issued a notice stating that, according to official sources from the two countries, the rebel army invading the province of Madrid was defeated by the government army at the Somma Pass and the Guadalajara area (both north of Madrid) yesterday, and has completely retreated. From Barcelona to Malaga, the entire coastline is in the hands of the government. Workers in the port of Bilbao in the northwest have resumed work (Havas dispatch on the 24th).

Barcelona One thousand members of the Catalonia Autonomous Province Militia left for the city of Zaragoza tonight to attack the rebel army. Currently, there are still 8,500 members of the militia who have been formed into three columns and will serve on the front lines very soon. The first column, consisting of 3,000 members, gathered in Catalonia Square this afternoon to prepare to depart. All the strong men who joined the army said goodbye to their families, and some young lovers came to see them off, whispering sweet words and being reluctant to part. The square suddenly presented a wartime scene. The second column, consisting of 2,000 members, gathered in the Tarragona area, mostly composed of a mixed force of security team infantry, gendarmes, and militiamen belonging to the People's Front. They have already left for the city of Zaragoza. The third column, consisting of 2,500 members, and another 1,000 members of the anti-fascist militia, are also preparing to depart. The above three columns are well-armed and have a magnificent military appearance, with a flight team leading the way and a light artillery team covering the rear. In addition, it is heard that the government can indeed control everything in the provinces of Andalusia and Cadiz. Only parts of the provinces of Aragon and Galicia are currently occupied by the rebel army. The government's air force is currently bombing Zaragoza. According to the pilots, they saw in the sky that the city of Yega had been captured by the government army (Havas dispatch on the 24th).

Hendaye, France The great chaos in Spain for days has caused the number of losses in life and property to increase daily, and the government army and the rebel party are still in a state of uncertainty as to who will win. Fierce fighting broke out in the Entellaza mountain pass today, and it continued all day long. The sound of artillery was heard here, and it could be clearly distinguished. Our agency's interviewer recently learned that there was no winner in this battle. The government army and the rebel army are still holding their original positions. This afternoon, several Spanish refugees fled to the village of Biarritz in France, with frightened faces and in a very miserable state. According to them, the battle was very fierce, and the number of gendarmes killed on the government army side was very large. At 5:00 in the afternoon, another group of refugees crossed the Bidasoa River and asked the French authorities to allow them to bring their livestock into the country. Another three gendarmes fled into French territory, claiming that when the rebel army came to attack, they were in the Entellaza mountain pass. After the battle, they were captured and taken to the Behobia area. After being briefly interrogated by the rebel army, they were ordered to be executed. Fortunately, they escaped and fled into France. In addition, according to news from San Sebastian, the station there was not burned down. The remaining rebel party fled into the Daria Hotel. The government army immediately surrounded it. For a time, the sound of gunfire was very dense around the hotel. Finally, the government army attacked the hotel and saw 27 members of the rebel party. All had committed suicide and were lying dead on the ground, knowing that they were no match and would rather shoot themselves than surrender. It is also heard that Salamanca and the port of Bilbao are currently still in the hands of the government army, and the local area is as peaceful as usual (Havas dispatch on the 24th).

Burgos General Mala, the commander-in-chief of the rebel army on the North Road, led 60,000 regular troops and volunteers and occupied the main road to Madrid today. As soon as the army on the South Road succeeds, it will attack the capital. Its advance team is searching for left-wing elements in the countryside. General Mala declared that several detachments of his troops are less than 40 miles from Madrid and are waiting for orders to attack, hoping that there will be no major bloodshed when the capital is occupied (National Telegraph on the 24th).

Rebel Headquarters in Tétouan, Morocco The leader of the Spanish rebel army, Franco, told the United Press reporter today that he is fighting according to the planned plan and is convinced that the revolutionary army will be able to achieve the final victory. The purpose of the revolution is to eliminate the power of Moscow. The revolutionary army has not encountered any difficulties so far, but the attitude of the navy has surprised him, saying that if the navy could be supplied with arms and food earlier, the navy could also join the revolution (National Telegraph on the 24th).

Prospects for the Five-Power Conference Britain Expresses Optimism Italy and Germany Have Not Yet Officially Replied 28

(London) Foreign Secretary Eden met with the German and Italian representatives this afternoon and informed them of the Locarno Conference held by the representatives of Britain, France, and Italy in London yesterday. The diplomatic representatives of the three countries in Germany and Italy also notified the governments of the two countries of the results of the three-nation conference and sent a letter of invitation for the five-nation conference this morning. Berlin issued a communique stating that Foreign Minister Neurath is not currently at the ministry, so the director of the political department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs met with the representatives of the three countries. It was not convenient to give an immediate reply at the time, only saying that they were willing to accept the document with interest and sympathy. It is also learned here that Germany and Italy are very satisfied with the acceptance of the three-nation proposal. The European situation has been deteriorating in recent years, and there is now hope for a turning point. Countries can now cooperate again to seek a general and lasting solution. In addition, according to a commentary by a diplomatic interviewer from a major British newspaper on the three-nation conference, yesterday can be called the anniversary of the turbulent Europe moving towards a new path to a solution. The newspapers here were moved and praised for the speed and consistency with which the three countries fulfilled the British government's real purpose. The location and date of the future five-nation conference will be resolved by the five countries through diplomatic channels (Reuters dispatch on the 24th).

(Berlin) Newspapers generally take a reserved attitude towards the communique issued by the representatives of Britain, France, and Belgium in London on the 23rd, but express hope, saying that if a peaceful construction plan is sought to be easily realized, then the future five-nation conference should only be attended by Western European countries. The Frankfurter Zeitung also issued an optimistic tone, "The achievements of this London talk are at least better than the first Locarno Conference on March 19. Since Germany abolished the Locarno Pact on March 7, after all parties were indignant, they have made various harsh demands. Up to this point, these harsh demands have been covered up by subsequent events and no longer maintain their original appearance. It is a pity that the three-nation communique still implicitly mentions "the situation caused by Germany's actions on March 7." This remnant of thought must be eradicated, and then the new Locarno Pact will be easier to establish." (Havas dispatch on the 25th).

(Rome) Italy has recently received invitations from Britain, France, and Belgium to participate in the future five-nation conference. Political figures here stated that Italy must wait a few days before replying. Informed sources said, "Once the conditions that Italy considers indispensable are put into practice, Italy will gladly re-enter into cooperation on European events." According to reports, Italy previously refused to participate in the Montreux Conference on the pretext that the Mediterranean Mutual Assistance Agreement had not yet been abolished. The so-called indispensable conditions here probably refer to this (Havas dispatch on the 24th).

(London) After the representatives of Britain, France, and Belgium held talks here on the 23rd, they immediately issued a communique. The German and Italian sides have commented on it. After hearing the news, the newspapers here still expressed optimism, but believed that before the construction of true peace in Europe could begin, there were still hidden difficulties that needed to be overcome urgently. The diplomatic reporter of the Manchester Guardian recently published a commentary, "It is natural for Germany and Italy to still have doubts about this communique. However, the hostile attitude expressed by each country is not as severe as generally expected. As for the last paragraph of this communique, which advocates that in addition to the five countries, other countries should also be able to participate in future conferences, Germany believes that there is still room for discussion, because this statement is equivalent to inviting Soviet Russia to participate in the conference." (Havas dispatch on the 25th).

The Future of the Hirota Cabinet (6) 29

— Jia He

Currently, the direct confrontation between the military and Hirota is not about any other issue, but about the expansion of the Investigation Bureau's authority, the establishment of a minister without portfolio as a result, and the reform of the administrative structure. When the Cabinet Deliberation Council was abolished, many people thought this was a precursor to the Investigation Bureau's elevation, but that is not the case. The existence of the Cabinet Deliberation Council was to strengthen the cabinet's function because the Seiyukai, the leading party at the time, adopted an opposition stance. The Hirota Cabinet, having obtained the support of political parties (albeit to a limited extent), naturally did not need such an organ. Moreover, after the loss of the two elders, Takahashi Korekiyo and Saito Makoto, it was impossible to find the same kind of people to fill the gap. Therefore, it was abolished with pleasure, which is not enough to be evidence for Yoshida Shigeru and others to celebrate. In fact, the Investigation Bureau, which the military hopes will have the power to initiate proposals and the power to budget, becoming a small cabinet within the cabinet, is still unknown. (The "Tokyo Asahi Shimbun" of March 20th still carried news of cabinet members opposing the strengthening of the Cabinet Investigation Bureau). Another message came that a minister without portfolio could be established according to the military's wishes, but this minister would not be at the beck and call of Yoshida Shigeru, the chief of the Miyakezaka district, but rather Prince Fumimaro Konoe, the president of the House of Peers (June 23rd "Chugai Shogyo Shimpo"); currently, all newspapers are frowning upon this matter, as if they cannot find the right person, then the establishment of a minister without portfolio will be difficult to pass in the cabinet meeting. By June 29th, the opposition between the Cabinet Investigation Bureau and the cabinet ministers became more obvious. This is because the former submitted to the cabinet meeting a plan to reform the administrative structure decided by all the councilors – namely, abolishing the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, merging the Ministries of Agriculture and Forestry, Commerce and Industry into the Ministry of Industry, merging Railways and Communications into the Ministry of Transport, and expanding the Bureau of Health into the Ministry of Health, reducing the original twelve ministries to ten – and the national policy proposal put forward by the three chiefs was also rejected by the cabinet members. Some cabinet members were unwilling to treat the proposal of all the councilors of the Investigation Bureau as a proposal, only allowing it to be kept for reference, ignoring Yoshida Shigeru's opposition. (June 30th "Chugai Shogyo Shimpo").

Cutting off the connection between the military and the young officers is something the young military officers could not tolerate. Their only hope is to elevate the Investigation Bureau. If that becomes a bubble, doesn't that mean throwing the military out of the political circle? The military only participates in politics in the cabinet meetings and can never win because it only occupies two seats. If the Investigation Bureau has expanded powers, with Yoshida Shigeru, the minister without portfolio and chief, at the top, and young officers and military-sent councilors at the bottom, it will naturally be able to achieve effective control. Now, the Hirota Cabinet not only does not satisfy their desires but wants them to retreat, which is absolutely unacceptable to the military. Therefore, at the end of June, General Terauchi "advised" Hirota, saying that there were too many "national policies" ("national policy overflow" was satirized by the press), and strongly supported Raimoki's "National Power Control Plan." As a result of being pressured by this "advice," Hirota broke his own rules and allowed the three chiefs to attend the cabinet meeting on July 3rd. Although the issue of administrative structure reform was not yet discussed, Raimoki's proposal was enough to cause a major dispute. Originally, Japan, due to its geographical location and lack of fuel resources, had a particularly developed electricity industry. Currently, all electricity is controlled by the five major electricity cartels: Tokyo Electric Power, Toho Electric Power, Daido Electric Power, Japan Electric Power, and Ujikawa Electric Power, intricately linked to the funds of the Mitsui, Mitsubishi, Sumitomo, and Yasuda zaibatsu. Due to the division of monopoly profits, major political tides often occur. The changes of cabinets during the Taisho era and the early Showa era were closely related to this. Later, in order to prevent mutual struggles from harming the rights of the zaibatsu, the relevant zaibatsu promoted their cooperation, and the "Electricity League Rules" came into being. This temporary truce did not eliminate internal disputes: Wako Shohachi of the Koshu-based zaibatsu, belonging to Tokyo Electric Power (a major figure in the Seiyukai), has always advocated "nationalization of electricity"; President Hayashi of Uji insists on "nationalization of power generation" and "privatization of power sales"; Koayashi Ichizo of the Mitsui zaibatsu uses the power of Tokyo to control the entire Japanese electricity industry, demanding the "merger of the five major electric power companies." These claims, backed by the respective zaibatsu, are still lurking in the minds of the heads of each electricity cartel. Now, due to the military's demands (which are quite beneficial to industrialists), they are accepting Yoshida Shigeru's nationalization proposal, which stipulates that ownership is held by investors and operating rights belong to the government, which is actually depriving the zaibatsu of their monopoly profits. Even the executives of the Minseito (which has close ties to Toho Electric Power) have taken an opposing stance, and other voices of opposition are spreading throughout the country. We do not know what Raimoki is thinking, who has always been subsidized by Showa Electric Power (a subsidiary of Daido Electric Power). Currently, if Yoshida Shigeru's original plan is implemented without modification, it will obviously be harmful and not beneficial to the major zaibatsu. According to the instructions of past history, this will become a major cause of future political tides. If Hirota does not handle it properly, due to the discord among the cabinet members (there were already differences of opinion among the ministers at the cabinet meeting on July 3rd), the anger of the zaibatsu, the future of the cabinet is not optimistic.

Lees-Ross Returns to London, Advocates Foreign Investment in China 30

(London) Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, the British government's economic advisor, returned here today from China. Sir Richard Hopkins, representing the Treasury, Mr. Ronald, representing the Foreign Office, and others welcomed him at Victoria Station. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

Marseilles Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, the British government's economic advisor, who was dispatched to China for nearly a year, recently returned to the country, passing through here, and issued a statement saying that if the situation in the northern provinces of China can be resolved, and domestic peace can be maintained for a long time, then the country's finances can reach a good state. The Chinese government has made many efforts to revive its financial economy. At present, if foreign private sectors can actively invest to support the development of various enterprises, then the revitalization work will naturally see more rapid progress. He also said that the current urgent task is to reform the tariff system: (1) to reduce tax rates; (2) to curb smuggling. Regarding the second item, the Chinese government has already implemented strict punishment measures to promote its progress. Those who violate the law in the most serious circumstances will even be sentenced to death. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Analysis of the Spanish Situation, Internal Strife and International Relations, The Rebellion's Military Expenses are Provided by the Wealthy, Arms Supplies Involve France, Germany, and Italy, Warships of Various Countries are Dispatched to Escort Nationals 33

Gibraltar General Kindelan, the air force commander of the Spanish rebels, is an assistant to the rebel leader General Franco. He recently telegraphed the foreign ministers of Italy and Germany, asking them to forward a request to the British government to stop the Spanish government fleet from operating near the port of Gibraltar, so as not to endanger the port of Gibraltar when our army's aircraft conduct bombing. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Madrid The government recently broadcast a radio message saying that the money used by the rebels was supplied by financier March. March is a famous Spanish banker. When General Sanjurjo, the leader of the restoration party, started an incident in 1932, he secretly provided funds and was sentenced to imprisonment. He then found a way to escape and lived abroad. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Marseilles The Spanish ship Tarragona and torpedo ship No. 17 have recently arrived in this port, reportedly with secret missions. The Spanish consul in Marseilles met with the captains of each ship, but refused to make a statement. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Barcelona The French cruiser Duguay-Trouin arrived in this city today. Admiral Soustel also arrived on the ship and immediately went ashore to visit Mr. Companys, the president of Catalonia. The French Citroen car factory also sent a telegram to Mr. Companys, expressing its congratulations on the province's victory over the fascist rebels. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Paris) Regarding the French government's plan to supply arms to the Spanish Republican government, although the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has denied it, the right-wing newspapers here are still criticizing the People's Front government for not supplying arms to the Spanish People's Front government. Among them, "Le Journal" reported that "The Spanish government has purchased aircraft from France, the first batch totaling four, and the transaction has been completed. The country's chargé d'affaires, Castillo, has resigned because he refused to sign the check. The military attaché of the country's embassy, Mr. Barroso, and the consuls-general stationed in Marseilles and Bayonne have also resigned for the same reason. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Paris) The Spanish civil war has caused repercussions internationally. The French right-wing newspapers are still continuing to attack the People's Front government for not supplying arms, aircraft, aircraft grenade launchers, field guns, and other military supplies to the Spanish People's Front government. Their rhetoric is becoming increasingly blatant. "Le Peuple", the organ of the orthodox Socialist Party, also published a message from Antwerp, Belgium, stating that General Franco, the commander-in-chief of the Spanish rebels, had purchased 24 aircraft from Italy. "The Italian government is eager to assist the Spanish right-wingers and establish a fascist system, thereby profiting from it and establishing hegemony in the Mediterranean." (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Paris) Regarding the French government's plan to supply arms and aircraft to the Spanish Republican government, "L'Intransigeant" reported that France and Spain have been in talks on the issue of purchasing arms, but deliveries have not yet begun. In addition, the Spanish government also requested the supply of 20,000 aircraft bombs, 50 machine guns, 8 75mm field guns, and 13 million rounds of ammunition. According to a message from the port of Bordeaux, the airmail plane that flew from Madrid to Paris a few days ago carried ten Spanish air force personnel. After landing at the port, it continued to fly to the capital. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Paris) Castillo, the Spanish chargé d'affaires in France, has resigned due to the country's government purchasing arms from France, and made a statement to the press, stating, "Regarding my resignation, the reports in various newspapers are inconsistent. I really have to issue a brief statement to clarify the truth. Since taking office, I have been deeply grateful for the preferential treatment I have received from the French government. I have always served the republican government of my country, including the current government, with loyalty. Now, driven by my conscience, I am unwilling to purchase foreign arms to kill my compatriots, so I have to resign. I don't want to say more than that." Afterwards, the Spanish embassy issued a statement firmly denying what Castillo said, and said that Castillo's false statements were a violation of diplomatic customs. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Paris) The cabinet is scheduled to hold an extraordinary cabinet meeting at the presidential palace this afternoon. This move is related to the Spanish situation. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(London) The Manchester Guardian recently commented on the Spanish situation, stating that the arms used by the rebels in the country, especially the rebels in Morocco, mostly came from Italy. In addition, German power is very strong in the Balearic Islands of Spain in the Mediterranean. If the rebels succeed in this Spanish rebellion, Germany can obtain the concession of the Balearic Islands. Therefore, the victory of the rebels is considered beneficial by Germany. Not only that, but if the rebels succeed, the situation will take on a new look, making it easier for Germany to operate in Western Europe. Germany already has many National Socialist Party branches in Spain, and its organization is very complete. In recent weeks, Germans have often gone to the country to strengthen its power. At the same time, German personnel are secretly deployed in the area, using the name of diplomacy and education as a cover for political or military espionage, and their organization is also very powerful. As for Morocco, it is most concerned by Germany. If the rebels win, Germany can not only obtain territorial concessions there, but also gain a foothold in North Africa. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(London) Although the Spanish government claims that Madrid is no longer in danger of being occupied by the rebels, according to the contradictory news received here today, the truth about the Spanish capital is confusing. Although railway and highway traffic in the area has been disrupted, there is no shortage of food for the people. Many British women and children in Madrid have been provided with food and accommodation by the British Embassy, which has also requested the Spanish government authorities to provide full protection for British nationals. The situation in Barcelona is still quite tense, but according to news received today, the local authorities have brought to justice those who have committed arson. It is reported that these villains mostly live in the city's major hotels and clubs. The British warship stationed in Barcelona has taken most of the British women and children and several American nationals aboard. However, most British women have decided to stay on shore with their husbands. Although food prices have risen sharply, they can still be purchased. A few newspapers also resumed publication for the first time yesterday. Two British destroyers that arrived in San Sebastian yesterday have left the country with more than 300 nationals. Another British destroyer has set sail for La Manga to transport another group of British nationals. Several British and American nationals in Tarragona were evacuated yesterday on a British destroyer. The remaining British warships are actively transporting nationals at various ports. There have been few injuries to foreigners during this disturbance. The only major incident is that the wife of the Norwegian consul in San Sebastian was seriously injured by a gunshot while looking out the window. In addition, a British student was also injured in San Sebastian. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

Warships are now rushing to the area and other three towns to rescue foreigners. Two British destroyers have rescued many British nationals from San Sebastian. Another three British destroyers, carrying 150 British nationals from Barcelona, have arrived in Marseilles. (London) The governments of Italy and Germany have both sent warships to Spain to protect their nationals. Upon hearing the news, political figures here have expressed great concern about the situation in Spain and fear that the arrival of Italian and German warships in the rebel areas of Spain will cause serious accidents and have an impact internationally. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

(Paris) Navy Minister Gasnier issued a statement to the newspapers tonight, saying that the French destroyer L'Indomptable had carried 300 French and other nationals at 5 pm this afternoon from the port of San Sebastian in Spain back to Saint-Jean-de-Luz, France. For those foreigners who did not have time to leave on this ship, another gunboat will be sent to transport them tomorrow. British Scientific Luminary Sir Henry Wellcome Passes Away 35

(London) Sir Henry Wellcome, the renowned British scientist, archaeologist, ethnologist, and author, passed away today due to illness. Wellcome was the current chairman of the Wellcome Trust Board of Trustees and the founder and director of the Wellcome Research Institute, the Historical Medical Museum, and the Scientific Research Bureau. In 1913, Wellcome made the Scientific Research Institute available to the government. In 1914, he established a special committee to study and improve the design and construction of military ambulances. In the same year, he created a mobile chemical microbial experiment vehicle for use by the British Army Medical Corps on the battlefield. During the last World War, it proved practical and effective in both Palestine and Egypt. In 1901, Wellcome personally went to the upper reaches of the Nile River in British Egypt and Sudan for archaeological and ethnological exploration. He revisited the area in 1910 to continue his unfinished work. Wellcome also discovered the previously unknown ancient city ruins of the Upper Egyptians in several places. He then implemented excavation and research work in four of these locations, which was temporarily suspended due to the outbreak of the war. He was also a pioneer in aerial photography, using it as a tool to explore and measure various ancient city ruins and record excavation sites. In 1927, he established the Lady Stanley Maternity Hospital in Uganda, Central Africa. In 1905, he founded the Wellcome Hospital Pharmacy, both managed by church medical officers. Wellcome also established a publishing fund, managed by the Chinese Medical Association, to provide standard textbooks of medicine, surgery, and chemistry, translated into Chinese at low prices, making them easily accessible to Chinese students. Wellcome was also the vice-president of the Anthropological Institute, the vice-chairman of the Fine Arts Society, and a member of many other societies. (Reuters, 25th)

Soviet Russian Army Holds Large-Scale Maneuvers in September, British Military Officers to Attend 36

(London) The Soviet Russian Army is scheduled to hold large-scale maneuvers in September. The British government has decided to send two or three military officers and the British military attache to the Russian embassy to attend. This is the first time since the European War that British military officers have attended large-scale maneuvers in Russia. (Reuters, 25th)

Educational Broadcast Supplement

Secondary Education (Part 2) 39

— Liao Shicheng, Professor, Guanghua University, Shanghai

Three, Misunderstanding the Nature and Application of Learning

A middle school student won first prize in a civic knowledge test competition. He knew very clearly about the ideal responsibilities of a citizen. Everyone thought he was a good citizen. But a few months later, he was arrested by the police for doing something that harmed public order. Common criticism was that the student did not truly understand the responsibilities of a citizen. His words were empty. Closer examination reveals that the problem is not so simple. Historically, schools have only focused on intellectual understanding, assuming that it can encompass all of life, and have particularly neglected appreciative and emotional responses. Taking the above example, the school only provided intellectual learning and understanding responses, assuming that it could control emotional and moral environments. In reality, learning responses of this kind should emphasize emotions or appreciation, and attitudes and actions. Therefore, it is not only necessary to know what constitutes true learning, but also to know what kind of learning response is required in what situations in life. Matters without emotional influence can be controlled by intellectual learning, but in situations requiring action, mere intellectual responses are of no use.

Misunderstanding the nature and application of learning also has another negative impact. For example, English requires at least four teaching methods: grammar uses scientific methods, literature must use appreciative methods, composition is a literary art, and spelling requires the principle of practice. The difference between grammar and literature is like the difference between algebra and sports. Therefore, someone who teaches grammar well may not teach literature well. But now it is all called English, and the teaching methods are not differentiated, so how can it be good?

In addition to the above three misunderstandings, there is another major flaw in teaching, which is teaching too much and learning too little. Students in the classroom only listen to the teacher's explanations and rarely engage in activities themselves. In the future, efforts should be made to integrate teaching and learning, and a portion of teaching time should be extracted in each subject to guide students in self-study. It should be known that the efficiency of teaching depends not on the amount of teaching time, but on the proper use of time.

The most difficult issue to handle in secondary school education is moral education, but it is also the most important. The quality of a school's discipline affects the entire administration, and the quality of a student's character affects their entire life. Therefore, all countries attach great importance to moral education. Recently, the discipline of secondary schools in our country has improved compared to the past. However, the spirit of students being lazy, perfunctory, undisciplined, and decadent still exists. The reason for this is that schools in the past had mistaken views on moral education. In the past, schools treated teaching as one thing and moral education as another. Therefore, teachers only knew how to teach in class and did not care about students' behavior or thoughts. Students only knew how to study at school and regarded physical training and emotional cultivation as secondary matters. The accumulation of frost leads to hard ice - this situation has been long-standing!

Speaking of the academic atmosphere, we all admire the "public schools" in England. The reason why their academic atmosphere is good is because teaching and moral education are not separated. Whether in teaching, sports, or other aspects of life, the entire student is trained. Therefore, the relationship between teachers and students is harmonious. There is not a student who does not love their teachers and their school. German secondary schools have always been constrained, rigid, and focused on intellectualism, but since the rise of the youth movement, the national spirit and attitude have changed. The main aim of the youth movement is to break free from the constraints of the city and engage more with nature. Those who participated in the movement advocated organizing small groups, living a life of roaming and picnicking, in order to cultivate young people's independent ability, strong bodies, and establish group discipline and a spirit of mutual assistance. Their unanimous slogan is to love the motherland, love the people, and love the local customs and traditions. This movement not only brought about major changes in the minds and bodies of young people but also influenced educational principles and implementation. According to their view, knowledge is the foundation of culture, not the purpose of culture. Culture represents activity, will, creativity, and a balanced and harmonious personality. Therefore, the goal of education should not be to obtain knowledge as the only skill, but to develop all aspects of the individual: body, will, and emotions. The efficiency of education should not be tested by the standard of repeating teaching materials, but by whether students have the interest and ability to discover the truth of things.

From the above two examples, the trend of Chinese secondary schools is not to focus on the inculcation of knowledge, but on the cultivation of the whole personality. Although we are currently advocating the integration of teaching and moral education, there are some changes in the system and personnel, but in spirit, there is still separation. The main reason for the separation is that teachers in general cannot deeply understand the importance of the integration of teaching and moral education. Therefore, the emotions between teachers and students are distant, and the efficiency of education is minimal. Future education must integrate teaching and moral education, and regard the entire youth as the object of training, and regard serving society and dedicating oneself to the country as the goal of training.

The nation is in such a serious crisis that we do not want secondary schools to cultivate a group of young people who are self-serving and study dead books. We hope that every young person, after receiving secondary education, will have a strong physique and know about sexual hygiene; read books and understand principles, have rich common sense, applied skills, and be able to use their minds to study profound academic principles at any time; be strong-willed, not afraid of danger, have clear responsibilities, not be stubborn, obey the orders of the group, and abide by public discipline. Every young person has the spirit of reforming society and the determination to revive the nation. We know that the great problem of China lies not in its powerful neighbors, but in the lack of transformation of people's hearts and the lack of unity among the people. If these two problems are not corrected, even if we are fortunate enough to win a battle, the country will still face repeated crises. If people's hearts are gradually transformed and the people are gradually united, even if we succumb for a time, there will eventually be a day of revival. The responsibility of transforming people's hearts and uniting the people must be borne by young people who have received secondary education. Young people who have received secondary education must start with themselves in order to be able to shoulder this heavy responsibility.

A Brief Conversation with the Deposed King of Spain, Alfonso 40

(Paris) The deposed King of Spain, Alfonso, stated to a reporter from the Paris Evening News today that he does not want to return to the country immediately. He also said that if the leftist government continues to cling to power, this revolution will never end. He deeply hopes that Spain will break free from terror and killings as soon as possible. Only the failure of the leftist government can end the civil war and bring peace to Spain. This revolution is purely a national movement, that is, the positive action of the Royalists and right-wing Republicans to overthrow the leftist government. (National Telegraph, 24th)

Tianjin Customs Officers Responsible for Anti-Smuggling, Southern-Bound Smuggled Goods Aground, Jinpu Railway Losses Reach 400,000 41

(Tianjin) Smuggled goods going south from Tianjin have not been transported for five days. The No. 305 train south on the Jinpu Railway has resumed normal order every night, and passenger traffic remains constant. Since the forced loading and transportation of smuggled goods by train, the Jinpu Railway's passenger transport losses have averaged 1,500 yuan per day, and freight losses have exceeded 4,000 yuan, totaling around 400,000 yuan. Tianjin Customs officers will now resume responsibility for anti-smuggling matters, proceeding according to ministry orders, and will no longer relax. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Tianjin) Japanese nationals have stored a total of 300,000 bags of sugar in Tianjin. Only 15,000 bags have been shipped south this month so far, compared to the past average monthly sales of 56,000 bags. According to sales, it will take half a year to clear the stock. Recently, due to strict customs anti-smuggling efforts, the Japanese are losing more than 100,000 yuan per week. The price of a bag of sugar has fallen from 15.7 yuan to 14.5 yuan. Currently, Dalian has 400,000 bags of sugar in stock, and they are still worried about finding a market. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Nanjing) The Jinling Customs has successively seized a large number of smuggled goods such as sugar and rayon. After separate auctions, no tax-evading goods have been found recently. All anti-smuggling personnel have nothing to do and are now transferred to the northern section of Jinpu to continue working in various anti-smuggling sub-offices. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Nanjing) Since the central government promulgated the regulations on punishing the leakage of customs duties, the Jinpu Railway has strengthened its assistance to the customs in anti-smuggling efforts, making it even stricter. A large number of smuggled goods smuggled on various passenger cars on the railway, from late May to the end of June this year, various passenger cars forcibly loaded more than 10,000 pieces of smuggled goods without tickets at Tianjin East Station, with rayon, sugar, cigarette paper, and cloth being the main items. The average freight cost of these smuggled goods, based on reaching Jinan, has not been less than 30,000 yuan. In addition, the third-class carriages of passenger cars are filled with smuggled goods, and passengers boarding the train are often squeezed off the train and demand a refund. This loss averages 8,000 yuan per day. In addition, the sugar car in Jinan was robbed, resulting in a loss of more than 8,000 yuan. In recent days, due to the abundance of smuggled goods, legitimate goods of the same type transported north from Pukou have almost disappeared. In addition, due to overloading, vehicles are damaged, and windows and other items are destroyed. It is reported that the railway has suffered direct and indirect losses of more than 350,000 yuan in the past month. (Central News Agency, 25th)

(Xuzhou) Based on a tip-off, the customs stationed in Xuzhou and the Public Security Bureau discovered that the Fuyi Sugar Warehouse in Nanguan was smuggling 168 bags of white sugar. They had no tax documents and refused to report. On the 24th, the two agencies jointly sealed it up, and on the 25th, they handed it over to the Jinpu Railway to allocate a car to transport it to Shanghai for customs to handle. (Central News Agency, 25th)

Hengyuan and Beiyang Cotton Mills Still Managed by Chinese Merchants, News of Japanese Investment and Sale is Inaccurate 42

(Tianjin) Lu Longzhi, the manager of Hengyuan and Beiyang Cotton Mills, said that since Chengxin Trust Company has been operating the two cotton mills, Hengyuan has invested more than 700,000 yuan, and Beiyang will also invest 600,000 to 700,000 yuan due to the expansion of its business. Currently, the two mills' operations are still sufficient to maintain. The news of Japanese investment and sale is absolutely inaccurate. Previously, the spread of this news shocked the cotton industry in the north and south, and many people came to inquire. So far, there has been no conclusion to the reply. The cotton industry in North China is not unfeasible. Labor is cheap, fundraising is easy, and it is convenient to obtain raw materials. Sales can be entirely in the domestic market, which is incomparable to the Japanese cotton industry, which obtains raw materials from others and also needs to expand sales abroad. Past failures of the industry are due to their own lack of effort. At the moment, the fear of being oppressed is close to being a self-inflicted worry. Although the Huaxin and Baocheng mills have been sold, it cannot be determined who the buyer is. If the shareholders of the two mills are determined to take the lead, and if industrialists are willing to help, the future is still bright. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

Yongding River Water Continues to Rise, Exceeding the Highest Water Level in History, Fortunately, It Has Fallen Five Inches Last Night 43

(Tianjin) On the 25th, the water level at the Dugou Bridge on the Yongding River continued to rise by six inches, with rapid and turbulent flow. The River Defense Joint Prevention Association telegraphed the River Bureau to warn of danger. The people of Shuangkou Town went to the dike to defend it on the night of the 24th. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Beiping) The Lugouqiao telephone reported that the Yongding River water rose sharply to 18 feet on the 24th, which is the highest level in history. The water was turbulent. At 0:20 on the morning of the 25th, it continued to rise by 5 inches, and the water level increased to 18 feet and 5 inches, exceeding the highest water level in history by 5 inches. The dangerous situation is unprecedented. The Yongding River Affairs Bureau telegraphed the magistrates of eight counties along the river, including Tianjin, Yongqing, and Wanping, on the morning of the 25th, requesting them to quickly send personnel to assist the local construction patrol sections to closely defend. Fortunately, the river water dropped by one foot at 6:30 in the afternoon. As of 8:00 p.m., the water level was 17 feet and 5 inches, down 5 inches from yesterday. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Tianjin) Zhang Huanming, the chief of the fifth section of the North Canal, reported that the water level in the Tongxian section had risen sharply, with a water level of 6.6 meters, only 1.2 meters away from the dike. The waves of the lower dikes are flying over, and a dangerous situation is imminent. He requested that laborers be quickly assembled to rush to block it. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

Tianjin Municipal Organ Reorganization 44

(Tianjin) The reorganization of Tianjin's administrative organs was officially announced by the municipal government on the 25th and has been submitted to the Executive Yuan and the Hebei-Chahar Political Council for filing. The Public Utilities Bureau and the Health Bureau have been abolished. Public utilities will be handled by the Electricity Industry Supervision Office, and the municipal government will add a section to handle health affairs. The Social Affairs Bureau and the Education Bureau will be separated. Li Zaizhong, the director of the Health Bureau, will be transferred to become the director of the Social Affairs Bureau. Ling Mianzhi will be appointed as the director of the Education Bureau. Ma Xianfu will be the director of the Electricity Industry Supervision Office. All bureaus, offices, and sections will be abolished and established separately on August 1. Liu Xizhong, the director of the Public Works Bureau, resigned and did not take office. Zhang Zizhong went to Beiping to persuade him. If he still refuses, another person will be selected to take over. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Tianjin) Ma Yanzhong said that the municipal system reform is purely to save costs. In the future, it will jointly administer five bureaus: Public Security, Social Affairs, Education, Finance, and Public Works. The Health Bureau will be changed to a section, and Ji Wenlong will be appointed as the section chief. It will still be established separately at the original site. The section chief will take over on the 27th. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

Ministry of Finance Explains Regulations on the Transportation and Sales of Imported Goods 59

(Nanjing) The Jiangsu Provincial Business Federation telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, asking whether the regulations on inspecting the transportation and sales of imported goods should require stores that purchase goods and return them to Shanghai for exchange due to quality and color discrepancies to have a certificate from the industry association or chamber of commerce for transportation. The Ministry of Finance has now set three measures: (1) When a business needs to return goods for exchange to the place of origin, it should report to the industry association or chamber of commerce. If the association or chamber of commerce verifies that the business's original transportation and sales license is consistent, it will issue a certificate. If the original transportation and sales license has been submitted to the customs by the association, the association will verify that it is consistent with the original registration when the goods arrived and issue a certificate for transportation. (2) When distributed goods need to be returned, the business should issue a pledge to the industry association or chamber of commerce at the location of the business's branch and request a certificate. (3) The aforementioned certificate should be returned to the original issuer at any time after use. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

Jiangxi Province: Yumin Bank Embezzlement Case: Deputy Director and Others Embezzle Huge Sums; Responsible Parties Arrested After Discovery 69

Nanchang correspondence: A major embezzlement case has recently been discovered at the Jiangxi Provincial Yumin Bank, causing a stir throughout the entire province. The Jiangxi Yumin Bank originally had a capital stock of one million yuan, which was later handled by Director of the Provincial Department of Finance Wu Jiantao, responsible for establishing it as a provincial financial center. Wu immediately expanded the bank's official shares to two million yuan, appointing Liao Xinren as the bank director and Qian Yuqi, from the money industry, as the deputy director. It issued one-dime, two-dime, and five-dime auxiliary coins totaling one million yuan, with branch offices and agencies established throughout various counties and cities, serving as agents for the provincial treasury and sub-treasuries for grain collection and tax collection in various counties. The business grew daily. However, Qian, at this time, openly pursued private gain. Last year, he colluded with Wu Meisun, the branch manager of the Shanghai Yumin Bank, to embezzle bank funds and repeatedly engage in speculative transactions such as buying and selling government bonds, resulting in losses of hundreds of thousands of yuan. At the same time, Qian's Yishengheng Money Exchange, with a capital stock of tens of thousands of yuan, presented a facade of hundreds of thousands of yuan, relying on the Yumin Bank as its backing. As a result, the outside world criticized the Yumin Bank. Director Wu also felt uneasy. Later, Director Wu was transferred to Guangdong, and Secretary-General Liu took over the Department of Finance. Chen Wei took over the Yumin Bank and, after thoroughly investigating, understood the details of the embezzlement. The bank secretly reported to Provincial Chairman Xiong Shihui, who telegraphed Wu Meisun to come to the province from Shanghai, and arrested both he and Qian Yuqi, handing them over to the local court for trial. Qian's Yishengheng Money Exchange has also been sealed, and all account books have been submitted to the local court for review. It is rumored that the amount embezzled by Wu and Qian from the bank is approximately several hundred thousand, approaching one million yuan. However, authorities are currently secretly investigating the true situation in order to severely punish them in the future. (July 22)

Situation in North China: The Situation in the Midst of Dullness: Zhang Zizhong Arrives in Beiping to Report on the Tianjin Incident; Cao Rulin and Tang Erhe Still Express Intention to Resign; Japanese Side Eagerly Hopes for Realization of Economic Cooperation; In Chahar, Prince De Forced to Form Eight Divisions 70

Beiping correspondence: In the past week, Beiping has entered the hot season, although there have been two heavy rains, the heat has not diminished, only the mornings and evenings are relatively cool. Due to the heat, various military and government agencies have changed their office hours to operate from 7:00 AM to 12:00 PM. In the afternoon, personnel from various agencies seek medicine to alleviate the heat. Regarding the diplomatic corps, ambassadors, ministers, or chargés d'affaires have begun to go to Beidaihe for summer, so the situation seems rather dull for a time. However, amidst this dullness, Qi Xieyuan suddenly came to Beiping, and Shi Yousan took the post of political commissioner, which is noteworthy. Furthermore, regarding Tianjin, during this dullness, the Tianjin Security Team shot and killed Zhang Delu, a special agent of the Japanese police station. Afterward, on the 23rd, the Japanese military authorities in Tianjin made demands to the Tianjin municipal government for apology, compensation, punishment of the perpetrator, and guarantees, which were accepted. It is heard that the Japanese side requested 30,000 yuan in compensation, and the perpetrator and instigator, Zou Fengling, was handed over by the Japanese police station to the Tianjin Public Security Bureau for punishment on the 24th. Tianjin Mayor Zhang Zizhong, on the evening of the 24th, came to Beiping from Tianjin to meet with Song Zheyuan to report on the resolution of the incident. According to Zhang, "The demands made by the Japanese side after this incident were still reasonable, and our side also conducted negotiations based on reason, and fortunately, a satisfactory resolution was reached. I have come to report the process to Chairman Song. My feelings about this matter are that although the occurrence of this incident was unfortunate, it can prevent similar incidents from happening again in the future. I will return to Tianjin in two or three days in Beiping."

Regarding the situation of the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee, in terms of personnel, in addition to the change of the chief of political affairs and the assignment of Pan Yugui to prepare for the Cangzhou-Shijiazhuang Railway project, four new members, Cao Rulin, Tang Erhe, Liu Ruming, and Ge Dingyuan, were added. Cao and Tang have expressed their intention not to assume their positions in Tianjin and Beiping. On the 24th, the committee held its 12th regular meeting, which Cao and Tang did not attend, while Liu and Ge were present as observers. Pan also expressed his intention to resign from the Cangzhou-Shijiazhuang Railway project, but Song Zheyuan immediately retained him and, during the 12th regular meeting, temporarily proposed that the Transportation and Economic Committees properly draft measures for constructing the Cangzhou-Shijiazhuang Railway, which was passed. The two committees are preparing to start drafting jointly. As for the coming of Qi and Shi to Beiping, in addition to discussing matters that should be noted at present, the issue of the re-emergence of a certain important figure was also discussed, but it is understood that now is not the time.

The issue of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation is most concerned by the Japanese side, and they are eager to see it realized. Wang Kemin previously came to Beiping and had contact with various parties concerned, but they were all general discussions of opinions, and no concrete aspects were discussed. When Wang left Beiping, he said that he planned to return to Beijing by the end of the month, but according to what is known here, Wang may not be able to come north as scheduled, and the twists and turns are not easily known to outsiders. The general situation of the situation is still not stable.

Regarding northern Chahar, everything remains the same. It is rumored that Prince De has been forced to form eight divisions and is currently recruiting new soldiers. Three divisions have already been established. These three divisions are under the command of the traitor Li Shouxin, and the candidates for the division commanders of the eight divisions are also said to have been appointed, but the Mongolians staying in Beiping are still keeping it secret.

Japanese Embassy Military Attaché Takeo Imai met with European and American reporters on the 24th, saying that the weather is hot now, and it is a good opportunity for everyone to travel and avoid the heat, and he believes that there will not be any problems at this time, but there are still obstacles in the situation in Hebei and Chahar, and methods will be gradually found to remove them. (July 24)

Hebei Province Completes Rural Cleanup; Decides to Continue Summer Defense; Formulates Plan and Orders All Counties to Comply; Decides to Officially Begin on August 1st 71

Baoding correspondence: The Hebei Provincial Government, in order to consolidate local security in the province, specially requested the Department of Civil Affairs and the Security Department to jointly formulate a provincial rural cleanup plan, ordering all county governments to strictly comply. The main tasks included checking household registrations, organizing baojia (a system of mutual responsibility groups), and strengthening the county governments' capabilities to ensure smooth implementation. Chairman Song Zheyuan also ordered the troops stationed in various parts of the province to assist in the nearby areas. Since the start of the program, progress has been very rapid. The checking of household registrations and the organization of rural areas (five households form a neighborhood, five neighborhoods form a village, and two villages form a township) have been completed one after another, and reports have been sent to the province. At the same time as organizing rural areas, residents of each household have also signed mutual security pledges, with the five households in each neighborhood mutually guaranteeing each other and having the responsibility to supervise and report at any time. If illegal behavior is found in one household in a neighborhood and the other four households do not report it, then the other four households will also be subject to the same punishment. As a result, it is extremely difficult for illegal and unscrupulous elements to establish themselves locally, and the basic organization of the local people has formed an extremely sound and consolidated phenomenon. As for the organization of baojia, it is currently being carried out based on the results of the organization of rural areas. The provincial government has set a deadline of the end of August for completion, and the county governments are actively promoting it. In the future, after the baojia is organized, the local able-bodied men will receive considerable training, so that the local people will have sufficient self-defense capabilities. In the event of banditry, it will naturally be easier to eliminate, and the local people will have no chance to rebel. The provincial government has recently decided to carry out summer defense this year, as the rural cleanup work in various counties has been largely completed, but at this time when the green gauze screens are rising, it is inevitable that illegal elements will seize the opportunity to act. Furthermore, bandits have recently been frequently moving back and forth in the border areas of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan, and many bandits are also lurking in the deep reed ponds in the Wen'an and Ba County areas. In addition to the county governments and local troops increasing their efforts to suppress them, the Department of Civil Affairs and the Security Department have formulated a plan for implementing summer defense this year. Security Director Zhang Yunrong presented it to Chairman Song for approval, and it was approved to be implemented as planned. Originally, it was planned to convene a provincial security conference of county magistrates, administrative commissioners, and county defense corps leaders to instruct them on the steps to implement summer defense. However, due to the importance of local security in various counties, it was feared that a lack of leadership would allow bandits to take advantage of the situation, so it was decided to change the form of the meeting and separately communicate this summer defense plan to the county governments, administrative commissioners, and county defense corps leaders, ordering them to advance the plan nearby. The main contents of the summer defense plan can be divided into three aspects: First, allocate the police and regiment forces of each county so that they are evenly and effectively used; second, strengthen the anti-bandit military forces of each county; and third, establish contact methods for joint defense and joint patrols in the border areas of each county. The provincial government has now formally promulgated this summer defense plan, ordering all counties to begin preparations and to begin summer defense on August 1. The provincial government attaches great importance to the liaison for joint defense and joint patrols between counties, ordering all county governments to immediately take action to establish contact nearby. In the event of banditry, they must mutually attack and jointly suppress the bandits, and must not sit idly by and allow them to roam, causing the banditry to spread. If any county encounters bandits and does not establish contact and allows them to cross into neighboring counties, the county magistrate will be subject to dismissal. The provincial government has repeatedly ordered all county governments to comply. Now, all counties have prepared thoroughly and are ready to begin summer defense on August 1. (July 24)

China Agricultural Bank Expands Loan Scope in Anhui; Increases Agricultural Loan Offices with Low-Interest Mortgage Loans; Provides Funds to Build Provincial Grain Warehouses 72

Wuhu correspondence: The China Agricultural Bank has been providing agricultural loans in Anhui for several years, which has helped regulate the rural economy in various counties. The increase in agricultural products has also been rapid. The bank, in order to benefit the entire province and truly benefit agriculture, is cooperating with the Anhui Provincial Rural Cooperation Committee to handle rural loans in various counties and towns, expanding the loan scope. Regarding the construction of provincial and county grain warehouses, the Anhui Grain Warehouse Management Office has also been in contact with the bank, which will provide large amounts of funds to complete the construction as soon as possible in order to store food. This year, in more than sixty counties in Anhui, except for a small number of high-lying fields in the northwest and east that have been slightly affected by drought, the harvests are better than in previous years. This is the best phenomenon since the major flood of the past twenty years. In the future, when the harvest is complete, the surplus grain will be managed and stored in grain warehouses by the province, waiting for prices to rise before selling, in order to prevent market monopolies and affect the farmers' economy. In addition, in order to circulate rural finances in Anhui Province, the Agricultural Bank plans to increase the number of farmer loan offices in Anqing, Wuhu, Tunxi, and Lu'an. Farmers can mortgage their clothing and utensils, with the monthly interest rate temporarily set at 1.5%, and they will be given convenient access, which is only 60% of the interest rate of ordinary pawnshops. The Wuhu loan office has already begun preparations, renting the former Futai pawnshop on Heng Street as its location and is currently renovating it. It will soon be able to start lending. Staff will be sent to other places to prepare. (July 24)

Suzhou: Conflict Between Merchants and Police Outside Xumen 73

Outside the Xumen Wanning Bridge Main Street, around 9:00 PM on the 23rd, all the shops had closed, and the shop employees were cooling off in front of the shops. Changshu: Forgery of Grain Certificates Leads to Arrest 74

The West Counter Grain Office in our county recently discovered that someone was forging grain certificates and fraudulently collecting national taxes, which is no different from forging banknotes and harming national revenue. The forger Zhou Laosi has been arrested and detained, awaiting disposal. Zhou Laosi, 38 years old, was originally an employee of the West Counter Micro-Grain Office of the county government and was very familiar with the internal situation. Later, due to his addiction, he left his position this spring. Zhou, feeling bored at home, came up with a wild idea and changed the appearance of old certificates from 1934 to fake new certificates, going to Xiqiao to fraudulently collect taxes. Many people were deceived. It was only when the tax collection official went to collect the money that the matter was discovered. After investigating, it was found that Zhou was responsible. The county government attaches great importance to this matter.

Fugitive Smoker Wanted 75

Zhou Jingyu, an accountant in the Bureau of Education, was reported for smoking opium. After verification, it was proven. Wuxi: Silk Mill Strike Resolved 76

After the silk mill strike throughout Wuxi County was resolved, the factories have resumed work as usual. However, the female workers of the Yongtai and Yongchang factories outside the South Gate mistakenly believed rumors that the factory had no intention of genuinely improving treatment, so they successively went on strike starting on the 23rd. The factory said that if the workers could not understand the factory's difficulties, then they could only let them do as they pleased. Therefore, on the morning of the 24th, the workers were not taken back to the factory, causing some workers to have no work to do, and the two sides reached a stalemate. This also affected the Dingchang and Minfeng factories, which also did not work that day. The female workers specially appointed representatives to report to the General Labor Union. Cadre Zhu Ruoyu and staff from the Industrial Labor Union held an emergency meeting at Qingming Bridge Elementary School and then went to Yongtai to negotiate with Assistant Manager Xue Zukang. The Public Security Bureau, fearing that the workers would gather everywhere, sent police to protect the area. After negotiations, it was decided: (1) The factory will take the workers back to the factory as usual on the morning of the 25th; (2) Wages will be in accordance with the standards set by the county government; (3) A standard clock will be hung in the workshop, and work will be carried out according to the specified time; (4) The staff will change to a more friendly attitude towards the workers. After the above items were confirmed, the workers' representatives expressed their satisfaction and immediately returned to inform the female workers. Yesterday, they returned to work as usual, restoring the original state.

Fire on Tonghui Road 78

Wang Azhong's house, located at No. 8 Tonghui Road, Wuqiao South, outside the North Gate of our county, caught fire around 10:00 PM the night before due to carelessness, causing a great conflagration. At that time, there was a strong wind and heavy rain, so the god of fire took advantage of the wind and raged, spreading to the neighboring Pinxian Tea House, Gao Quanrong, Zhang Xianyuan, and 14 other households. After the firefighters from the North District, sections 3, 4, 6, 7, 9, and Ximen heard the alarm, they drove to the scene to put out the fire. It took about an hour to extinguish the fire, but the buildings in the area had been reduced to ashes. The total loss is estimated to be over 20,000 yuan. When the fire was raging, Wu Xianzai, a resident of No. 9, was burned on the face and arms when he escaped from the fire. His daughter, Yan Qiaoyun, jumped from the building and injured her buttocks. Fortunately, the injuries are minor, and there is no danger to life. In addition, the house of Yang Gouda, located at No. 21 Jia, Section 3, Xijingzhen, outside the East Gate, suddenly caught fire around 1:00 AM yesterday (25th) and could not be contained, spreading to Shengxi Wang Lingen, Gu Axi, Zhu Linshi, and the neighbors Yang Ahe, Mao Julin, Qin Jinpei, Yang Hongyi, and eight other households, with losses of over 10,000 yuan. Yang Gouda and Yang Hongyi suffered the greatest losses because they were both newlyweds, and all their belongings were not salvaged.

Changzhou: Nunnery Robbed, Two Thieves Caught 79

Ni Shengfu, the abbess of the Jinghui Nunnery in Huaidong Township, Fourth District of Wuyi County, was targeted by thieves because the nunnery had some assets. On the night of the 23rd, seven or eight bandits, each carrying weapons and flashlights, entered by scaling the wall from the north, tying up more than a dozen nuns, large and small, burning Shengfu's breasts with fire, and beating her indiscriminately for about an hour before fleeing with the stolen goods. They planned to divide the loot outside Xiaonanmen, and one of the thieves, while walking along Chunting Bridge on Xinfeng Road, was caught by a watchman. The watchman and the local police took him to the Fifth Police Station of the First Public Security Bureau. The thief, named Li Ben, confessed to the robbery of the nunnery. Another suspect, Zhang Wenzi, who harbored the thief, was arrested and, along with Li Ben, was sent to the First Public Security Bureau on the 24th for investigation.
